    <section class="section section-dark">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Our Story</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">The Blacksmith Market has evolved from a boutique distributor to one of the UK's most trusted wholesale partners for branded products.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="about-content">
                <div class="about-image animate-on-scroll">
                    <img src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1521791136064-7986c2920216?ixlib=rb-4.0.3&ixid=M3wxMjA3fDB8MHxwaG90by1wYWdlfHx8fGVufDB8fHx8fA%3D%3D&auto=format&fit=crop&w=1469&q=80" alt="Business meeting with product samples">
                </div>
                <div class="about-text animate-on-scroll">
                    <h3>Our Beginning</h3>
                    <p>Founded in 2018, The Blacksmith Market began with a clear vision: to modernize wholesale distribution by connecting quality manufacturers with multiple retail channels through data-driven decision making.</p>
                    <p>Our founders recognized that many excellent branded products struggled to reach their full potential in the UK market due to distribution challenges. By creating a more flexible, responsive distribution model, we've been able to help both manufacturers and retailers thrive.</p>
                    <p>Today, we're proud to be a registered UK business with a growing presence across multiple product categories and retail channels.</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We aim to respond to all supplier inquiries within 2-3 business days. During peak periods, it may take up to 5 business days. If your inquiry is urgent, please mention this in your message or follow up with a phone call.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What information should I include in my supplier inquiry?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>To help us evaluate your products efficiently, please provide detailed information about your product range, pricing structure, minimum order quantities, lead times, and any relevant certifications or compliance documentation. It's also helpful to share information about your current distribution channels and markets.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Do you work with manufacturers outside the UK?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Yes, we work with manufacturers from around the world. We have experience managing international supply chains and can provide guidance on UK import requirements, compliance standards, and market adaption as needed.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Is there a minimum order value or quantity requirement?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Our minimum order requirements vary by product category and are established on a case-by-case basis. We're flexible and work with suppliers of various sizes, from established brands to emerging manufacturers. We'll discuss specific requirements during our evaluation process.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

            <h1>Frequently Asked Questions</h1>
            <nav aria-label="breadcrumb">
                <ol class="breadcrumb">
                    <li class="breadcrumb-item"><a href="index.html">Home</a></li>

    <!-- FAQ Section -->
    <section class="section section-dark">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Common Questions About Our Services</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">Get answers to frequently asked questions about working with The Blacksmith Market, our distribution services, and partnership opportunities.</p>
            </div>
            
            <!-- General Questions -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>General Information</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What is The Blacksmith Market?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>The Blacksmith Market is a UK-registered wholesale distributor specializing in branded products across multiple categories including Home & Kitchen, Beauty & Personal Care, Toys & Games, Electronics, and Health & Wellness. We connect quality manufacturers with profitable retail channels through strategic product selection and efficient distribution.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Is The Blacksmith Market an e-commerce store?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>No, The Blacksmith Market is not an e-commerce store. We are a wholesale distributor that works directly with manufacturers and retailers. Our website serves to provide information about our services and establish credibility with potential business partners, but does not offer direct consumer sales.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What retail channels do you distribute through?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We distribute through multiple retail channels including online marketplaces (such as Amazon and eBay), specialty retailers, independent shops, department stores, and direct-to-consumer platforms. Our multi-channel approach ensures products reach the right consumers through the most effective retail environments.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- For Suppliers -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>For Suppliers & Manufacturers</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do I become a supplier for The Blacksmith Market?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>To become a supplier, please complete our <a href="contact.html">supplier inquiry form</a>. We'll review your information and contact you to discuss potential partnership opportunities. Our team evaluates products based on market potential, quality, pricing structure, and alignment with our product categories.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What are your typical order quantities?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>Our order quantities vary by product category, seasonality, and sales velocity. Initial orders typically range from 50-200 units per SKU for testing market response. For established products with proven sales, our regular orders can range from 200-1,000+ units depending on category and demand.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What are your payment terms?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We typically work with standard industry payment terms of Net 30 or Net 60 days. For new suppliers, we may start with a deposit and balance payment structure until the relationship is established. Long-term partners may qualify for more favorable terms as our relationship develops.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Do you require exclusive distribution rights?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>While we don't require exclusivity for all products, we may discuss exclusive arrangements for select categories or channels where we can demonstrate significant market penetration and sales potential. These arrangements are negotiated on a case-by-case basis to ensure they benefit both parties.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Do you work with international manufacturers?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>Yes, we work with manufacturers from around the world. We have experience managing international supply chains and can provide guidance on UK import requirements, compliance standards, and market adaptation. We're particularly interested in unique, high-quality products with strong market potential.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Product & Quality -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>Product Requirements & Quality</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What types of products do you distribute?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We specialize in branded products across several categories:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li><strong>Home & Kitchen:</strong> Cookware, organization solutions, home décor, and cleaning innovations</li>
                                <li><strong>Beauty & Personal Care:</strong> Skincare, haircare, cosmetics, and beauty tools</li>
                                <li><strong>Toys & Games:</strong> Educational toys, board games, plush toys, and creative play items</li>
                                <li><strong>Electronics:</strong> Audio accessories, charging solutions, and smart home products</li>
                                <li><strong>Health & Wellness:</strong> Fitness accessories, massage products, and self-care items</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We're particularly interested in innovative, high-quality products that address specific consumer needs or provide unique solutions.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What quality standards do your products need to meet?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>All products must meet UK safety and quality standards, including relevant certifications (e.g., CE/UKCA marking). We conduct thorough quality assessments before onboarding new products, evaluating factors such as:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Material quality and durability</li>
                                <li>Manufacturing consistency</li>
                                <li>Packaging quality and presentation</li>
                                <li>Compliance with UK regulations</li>
                                <li>User experience and functionality</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We work with suppliers who demonstrate a consistent commitment to quality control and continuous improvement.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What documentation do you need from suppliers?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We require comprehensive product documentation including:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Detailed product specifications and features</li>
                                <li>High-resolution product images (including lifestyle and packaging)</li>
                                <li>Safety certifications relevant to the UK market</li>
                                <li>User manuals and instruction guides</li>
                                <li>Warranty information</li>
                                <li>Country of origin and manufacturing details</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>For international suppliers, we also need relevant export documentation and evidence of ethical manufacturing practices.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Operations & Logistics -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>Operations & Logistics</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do you handle product returns and warranties?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We work with suppliers to establish clear return and warranty policies that meet UK consumer expectations while being fair to all parties. Typically, we handle minor returns through our own processes but coordinate with suppliers on larger warranty issues or product defects. Our goal is to minimize returns through quality product selection and clear consumer communication.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What is your shipping and logistics process?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We operate a streamlined logistics system from our UK warehouse facilities. Our process includes:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Coordinating inbound shipments from suppliers</li>
                                <li>Quality control inspection upon receipt</li>
                                <li>Inventory management and storage</li>
                                <li>Order processing for various retail channels</li>
                                <li>Packaging and outbound shipping to retailers or direct to consumers</li>
                                <li>Returns processing and management</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We work with reliable shipping partners to ensure efficient delivery throughout the UK and internationally when required.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do you manage inventory and forecasting?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We use advanced inventory management systems and data analytics to optimize stock levels and forecast demand. Our approach includes:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Regular sales data analysis across all channels</li>
                                <li>Seasonal demand forecasting</li>
                                <li>Just-in-time inventory management to minimize carrying costs</li>
                                <li>Proactive communication with suppliers about upcoming needs</li>
                                <li>Demand planning for promotional periods and peak seasons</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>This systematic approach ensures we maintain optimal inventory levels while minimizing stockouts and overstock situations.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

                <div class="title-underline"></div>

                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">02</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Product Evaluation</h3>
                        <p>Our product team evaluates your offerings based on quality, market potential, pricing structure, and alignment with our product categories.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">03</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Partnership Discussion</h3>

                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">04</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Initial Order</h3>
                        <p>We place a starter order to introduce your products to our distribution channels and assess market response.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">05</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Performance Review</h3>
                        <p>After the initial period, we review sales performance and consumer feedback to optimize our distribution strategy.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">06</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Growth Planning</h3>

                    </div>

                    <div class="criteria-icon">
                        <i class="fas fa-medal"></i>
                    </div>
                    <h3>Product Quality</h3>
                    <p>High-quality products that meet or exceed UK consumer expectations and safety standards. We carefully evaluate durability, functionality, and overall quality.</p>
                </div>
                <div class="criteria-card animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="criteria-icon">
                        <i class="fas fa-lightbulb"></i>
                    </div>

                    <p>Products that offer unique features, solve consumer problems, or bring fresh concepts to established categories. Innovation helps products stand out in competitive markets.</p>
                </div>

                    <div class="criteria-icon">

                    <p>Price points that allow for competitive retail positioning while maintaining healthy margins for all parties in the distribution chain.</p>

                    <div class="criteria-icon">
                        <i class="fas fa-box"></i>
                    </div>

                    <p>Retail-ready packaging that protects products, communicates value, and enhances shelf presence. Packaging should meet UK labeling requirements.</p>

                    <div class="criteria-icon">

    <!-- FAQ Section -->
    <section class="section section-light">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">Common questions from potential supplier partners.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq-container">
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What retail channels do you distribute through?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We distribute products through multiple channels including online marketplaces (Amazon, eBay), specialty retailers, independent shops, and direct-to-consumer platforms. Our multi-channel approach allows us to place products where they're most likely to succeed based on category, price point, and target audience.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What are your typical order quantities?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Our order quantities vary by product category, seasonality, and sales velocity. Initial orders typically range from 50-200 units per SKU for testing market response. For established products with proven sales, our regular orders can range from 200-1,000+ units depending on category and sales volume.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What are your payment terms?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We typically work with standard industry payment terms of Net 30 or Net 60 days. For new suppliers, we may start with a deposit and balance payment structure until the relationship is established. Long-term partners may qualify for more favorable terms as our relationship develops.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Do you require exclusive distribution rights?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>While we don't require exclusivity for all products, we may discuss exclusive arrangements for select categories or channels where we can demonstrate significant market penetration and sales potential. These arrangements are negotiated on a case-by-case basis to ensure they benefit both parties.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>How do you handle product returns and warranties?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We work with suppliers to establish clear return and warranty policies that meet UK consumer expectations while being fair to all parties. Typically, we handle minor returns through our own processes but coordinate with suppliers on larger warranty issues or product defects.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What documentation do you need from suppliers?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We require standard product documentation including detailed specifications, high-resolution images, safety certifications relevant to the UK market (e.g., CE/UKCA marking), user manuals, and any required compliance documentation. For international suppliers, we also need export documentation and proof of ethical manufacturing practices.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

    <!-- Privacy Policy Content -->
    <section class="section section-dark">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="legal-content">
                <div class="last-updated">
                    <p>Last Updated: April 1, 2025</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>1. Introduction</h2>
                    <p>The Blacksmith Market Ltd. ("we," "our," or "us") is committed to protecting your privacy and the security of your personal information. This Privacy Policy outlines how we collect, use, store, and protect the information we collect from you when you use our website (www.theblacksmithmarket.co.uk), contact us, or engage with us as a supplier, partner, or other business relationship.</p>
                    <p>We operate in compliance with applicable data protection laws, including the UK General Data Protection Regulation (UK GDPR) and the Data Protection Act 2018. By using our website or providing us with your information, you consent to the collection and use of information in accordance with this policy.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>2. Information We Collect</h2>
                    <p>We may collect the following types of information:</p>
                    
                    <h3>2.1 Personal Information</h3>
                    <p>We may collect personal information that you provide to us, including:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Contact information (name, email address, phone number, business address)</li>
                        <li>Company details (company name, role, industry)</li>
                        <li>Communication preferences</li>
                        <li>Information provided in communications with us (email correspondence, inquiry forms, etc.)</li>
                    </ul>
                    
                    <h3>2.2 Automatically Collected Information</h3>
                    <p>When you visit our website, we may automatically collect certain information, including:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>IP address</li>
                        <li>Browser type and version</li>
                        <li>Operating system</li>
                        <li>Device information</li>
                        <li>Pages visited and navigation patterns</li>
                        <li>Time and date of visits</li>
                        <li>Referral sources</li>
                    </ul>
                    
                    <h3>2.3 Business Relationship Information</h3>
                    <p>If you engage with us as a supplier, partner, or in another business capacity, we may collect additional information necessary for our business relationship, including:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Business and financial information</li>
                        <li>Product details and specifications</li>
                        <li>Transaction history</li>
                        <li>Contract and agreement details</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>3. How We Use Your Information</h2>
                    <p>We use the information we collect for various purposes, including:</p>
                    
                    <h3>3.1 Providing Our Services</h3>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Responding to your inquiries and providing information about our services</li>
                        <li>Processing and managing business relationships</li>
                        <li>Fulfilling our contractual obligations</li>
                        <li>Communicating with you about our services, products, and operations</li>
                    </ul>
                    
                    <h3>3.2 Improving Our Website and Services</h3>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Analyzing website usage to improve user experience</li>
                        <li>Debugging and fixing technical issues</li>
                        <li>Developing new features and services</li>
                        <li>Conducting research and analysis to enhance our business operations</li>
                    </ul>
                    
                    <h3>3.3 Marketing and Communication</h3>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Sending relevant industry insights, updates, and marketing communications (where you have opted in)</li>
                        <li>Inviting you to events or webinars that may be of interest</li>
                        <li>Providing information about new products or services</li>
                    </ul>
                    
                    <h3>3.4 Legal and Regulatory Compliance</h3>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Complying with applicable laws, regulations, and legal processes</li>
                        <li>Enforcing our terms, conditions, and policies</li>
                        <li>Protecting our rights, privacy, safety, or property</li>
                        <li>Preventing, investigating, and addressing potential fraud or security issues</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>4. Legal Basis for Processing</h2>
                    <p>We process your personal information based on one or more of the following legal grounds:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li><strong>Consent:</strong> Where you have given us explicit consent to process your information for specific purposes.</li>
                        <li><strong>Contractual Necessity:</strong> Where processing is necessary for the performance of a contract to which you are a party or to take steps at your request before entering into a contract.</li>
                        <li><strong>Legitimate Interests:</strong> Where processing is necessary for our legitimate interests, provided those interests do not override your fundamental rights and freedoms.</li>
                        <li><strong>Legal Obligation:</strong> Where processing is necessary for compliance with a legal obligation to which we are subject.</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>5. Data Sharing and Disclosure</h2>
                    <p>We may share your information with:</p>
                    
                    <h3>5.1 Service Providers</h3>
                    <p>We may share your information with third-party service providers who perform services on our behalf, such as web hosting, data analysis, payment processing, IT services, customer service, email delivery, and other similar services. These providers are contractually obligated to use your information only as necessary to provide these services to us.</p>
                    
                    <h3>5.2 Business Partners</h3>
                    <p>In certain circumstances, and with your consent where required, we may share information with our business partners who offer products or services we believe may be of interest to you.</p>
                    
                    <h3>5.3 Legal Requirements</h3>
                    <p>We may disclose your information if required to do so by law or in response to valid requests from public authorities (e.g., courts or government agencies).</p>
                    
                    <h3>5.4 Business Transfers</h3>
                    <p>If we are involved in a merger, acquisition, or sale of all or a portion of our assets, your information may be transferred as part of that transaction. We will notify you of any such change and outline your choices in that event.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>6. Data Security</h2>
                    <p>We implement appropriate technical and organizational measures to help protect your personal information from unauthorized access, misuse, or accidental loss. These measures include:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Data encryption</li>
                        <li>Secure data storage</li>
                        <li>Regular security assessments</li>
                        <li>Access controls</li>
                        <li>Staff training on data protection practices</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>While we take reasonable steps to protect your information, no method of transmission over the Internet or electronic storage is 100% secure. Therefore, we cannot guarantee absolute security.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>7. Data Retention</h2>
                    <p>We retain your personal information for as long as necessary to fulfill the purposes for which it was collected, including for the purposes of satisfying any legal, accounting, or reporting requirements. To determine the appropriate retention period, we consider:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>The amount, nature, and sensitivity of the personal information</li>
                        <li>The potential risk of harm from unauthorized use or disclosure</li>
                        <li>The purposes for which we process the information and whether we can achieve those purposes through other means</li>
                        <li>Applicable legal, regulatory, or contractual requirements</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>8. Cookies and Similar Technologies</h2>
                    <p>Our website uses cookies and similar technologies to enhance your browsing experience, analyze site usage, and assist in our marketing efforts. Cookies are small text files that are placed on your device when you visit a website.</p>
                    <p>We use the following types of cookies:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li><strong>Essential cookies:</strong> Necessary for the functioning of our website.</li>
                        <li><strong>Analytical/performance cookies:</strong> Allow us to recognize and count visitors and see how they move around our website.</li>
                        <li><strong>Functionality cookies:</strong> Enable us to personalize your experience on our website.</li>
                        <li><strong>Targeting cookies:</strong> Record your visit to our website, the pages you visit, and the links you follow to improve the relevance of our communications.</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>You can set your browser to refuse all or some browser cookies or to alert you when websites set or access cookies. However, if you disable or refuse cookies, some parts of our website may become inaccessible or not function properly.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>9. Your Rights</h2>
                    <p>Depending on your location and applicable law, you may have the following rights regarding your personal information:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li><strong>Access:</strong> The right to request a copy of the personal information we hold about you.</li>
                        <li><strong>Rectification:</strong> The right to request correction of inaccurate or incomplete information.</li>
                        <li><strong>Erasure:</strong> The right to request deletion of your personal information in certain circumstances.</li>
                        <li><strong>Restriction:</strong> The right to request the restriction of processing of your personal information in certain circumstances.</li>
                        <li><strong>Data Portability:</strong> The right to receive your personal information in a structured, commonly used, and machine-readable format.</li>
                        <li><strong>Objection:</strong> The right to object to processing of your personal information in certain circumstances.</li>
                        <li><strong>Withdraw Consent:</strong> The right to withdraw your consent where we process your information based on consent.</li>
                        <li><strong>Complaint:</strong> The right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority.</li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>To exercise any of these rights, please contact us using the information provided in the "Contact Us" section below.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>10. International Data Transfers</h2>
                    <p>We primarily process and store your information within the United Kingdom. However, in some cases, your information may be transferred to, stored, or processed in countries outside the UK, particularly when we use third-party service providers based in other countries.</p>
                    <p>When transferring data outside the UK, we ensure appropriate safeguards are in place to protect your information, such as standard contractual clauses approved by relevant data protection authorities, binding corporate rules, or other legally accepted mechanisms.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>11. Changes to This Privacy Policy</h2>
                    <p>We may update this Privacy Policy from time to time to reflect changes in our practices or for other operational, legal, or regulatory reasons. When we make changes, we will update the "Last Updated" date at the top of this policy and take appropriate measures to inform you, consistent with the significance of the changes we make.</p>
                    <p>We encourage you to review this Privacy Policy periodically to stay informed about how we are protecting your information.</p>
                </div>
                
                <div class="legal-section">
                    <h2>12. Contact Us</h2>
                    <p>If you have any questions, concerns, or requests regarding this Privacy Policy or our data practices, please contact us at:</p>
                    <div class="contact-details">

    <section class="section section-dark">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Our Story</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">The Blacksmith Market has evolved from a boutique distributor to one of the UK's most trusted wholesale partners for branded products.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="about-content">
                <div class="about-image animate-on-scroll">
                    <img src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1521791136064-7986c2920216?ixlib=rb-4.0.3&ixid=M3wxMjA3fDB8MHxwaG90by1wYWdlfHx8fGVufDB8fHx8fA%3D%3D&auto=format&fit=crop&w=1469&q=80" alt="Business meeting with product samples">
                </div>
                <div class="about-text animate-on-scroll">
                    <h3>Our Beginning</h3>
                    <p>Founded in 2018, The Blacksmith Market began with a clear vision: to modernize wholesale distribution by connecting quality manufacturers with multiple retail channels through data-driven decision making.</p>
                    <p>Our founders recognized that many excellent branded products struggled to reach their full potential in the UK market due to distribution challenges. By creating a more flexible, responsive distribution model, we've been able to help both manufacturers and retailers thrive.</p>
                    <p>Today, we're proud to be a registered UK business with a growing presence across multiple product categories and retail channels.</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">Common questions about contacting and working with The Blacksmith Market.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="faq-container">
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>How quickly will I receive a response to my inquiry?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We aim to respond to all supplier inquiries within 2-3 business days. During peak periods, it may take up to 5 business days. If your inquiry is urgent, please mention this in your message or follow up with a phone call.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What information should I include in my supplier inquiry?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>To help us evaluate your products efficiently, please provide detailed information about your product range, pricing structure, minimum order quantities, lead times, and any relevant certifications or compliance documentation. It's also helpful to share information about your current distribution channels and markets.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Do you work with manufacturers outside the UK?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Yes, we work with manufacturers from around the world. We have experience managing international supply chains and can provide guidance on UK import requirements, compliance standards, and market adaption as needed.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Is there a minimum order value or quantity requirement?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Our minimum order requirements vary by product category and are established on a case-by-case basis. We're flexible and work with suppliers of various sizes, from established brands to emerging manufacturers. We'll discuss specific requirements during our evaluation process.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>

            <h1>Frequently Asked Questions</h1>
            <nav aria-label="breadcrumb">
                <ol class="breadcrumb">

    <!-- FAQ Section -->
    <section class="section section-dark">
        <div class="container">
            <div class="section-header">
                <h2 class="section-title">Common Questions About Our Services</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">Get answers to frequently asked questions about working with The Blacksmith Market, our distribution services, and partnership opportunities.</p>
            </div>
            
            <!-- General Questions -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>General Information</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What is The Blacksmith Market?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>The Blacksmith Market is a UK-registered wholesale distributor specializing in branded products across multiple categories including Home & Kitchen, Beauty & Personal Care, Toys & Games, Electronics, and Health & Wellness. We connect quality manufacturers with profitable retail channels through strategic product selection and efficient distribution.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Is The Blacksmith Market an e-commerce store?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>No, The Blacksmith Market is not an e-commerce store. We are a wholesale distributor that works directly with manufacturers and retailers. Our website serves to provide information about our services and establish credibility with potential business partners, but does not offer direct consumer sales.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What retail channels do you distribute through?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We distribute through multiple retail channels including online marketplaces (such as Amazon and eBay), specialty retailers, independent shops, department stores, and direct-to-consumer platforms. Our multi-channel approach ensures products reach the right consumers through the most effective retail environments.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- For Suppliers -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>For Suppliers & Manufacturers</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do I become a supplier for The Blacksmith Market?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>To become a supplier, please complete our <a href="contact.html">supplier inquiry form</a>. We'll review your information and contact you to discuss potential partnership opportunities. Our team evaluates products based on market potential, quality, pricing structure, and alignment with our product categories.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What are your typical order quantities?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>Our order quantities vary by product category, seasonality, and sales velocity. Initial orders typically range from 50-200 units per SKU for testing market response. For established products with proven sales, our regular orders can range from 200-1,000+ units depending on category and demand.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What are your payment terms?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We typically work with standard industry payment terms of Net 30 or Net 60 days. For new suppliers, we may start with a deposit and balance payment structure until the relationship is established. Long-term partners may qualify for more favorable terms as our relationship develops.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Do you require exclusive distribution rights?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>While we don't require exclusivity for all products, we may discuss exclusive arrangements for select categories or channels where we can demonstrate significant market penetration and sales potential. These arrangements are negotiated on a case-by-case basis to ensure they benefit both parties.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>Do you work with international manufacturers?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>Yes, we work with manufacturers from around the world. We have experience managing international supply chains and can provide guidance on UK import requirements, compliance standards, and market adaptation. We're particularly interested in unique, high-quality products with strong market potential.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Product & Quality -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>Product Requirements & Quality</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What types of products do you distribute?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We specialize in branded products across several categories:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li><strong>Home & Kitchen:</strong> Cookware, organization solutions, home décor, and cleaning innovations</li>
                                <li><strong>Beauty & Personal Care:</strong> Skincare, haircare, cosmetics, and beauty tools</li>
                                <li><strong>Toys & Games:</strong> Educational toys, board games, plush toys, and creative play items</li>
                                <li><strong>Electronics:</strong> Audio accessories, charging solutions, and smart home products</li>
                                <li><strong>Health & Wellness:</strong> Fitness accessories, massage products, and self-care items</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We're particularly interested in innovative, high-quality products that address specific consumer needs or provide unique solutions.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What quality standards do your products need to meet?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>All products must meet UK safety and quality standards, including relevant certifications (e.g., CE/UKCA marking). We conduct thorough quality assessments before onboarding new products, evaluating factors such as:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Material quality and durability</li>
                                <li>Manufacturing consistency</li>
                                <li>Packaging quality and presentation</li>
                                <li>Compliance with UK regulations</li>
                                <li>User experience and functionality</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We work with suppliers who demonstrate a consistent commitment to quality control and continuous improvement.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What documentation do you need from suppliers?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We require comprehensive product documentation including:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Detailed product specifications and features</li>
                                <li>High-resolution product images (including lifestyle and packaging)</li>
                                <li>Safety certifications relevant to the UK market</li>
                                <li>User manuals and instruction guides</li>
                                <li>Warranty information</li>
                                <li>Country of origin and manufacturing details</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>For international suppliers, we also need relevant export documentation and evidence of ethical manufacturing practices.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Operations & Logistics -->
            <div class="faq-category">
                <h2>Operations & Logistics</h2>
                <div class="faq-container">
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do you handle product returns and warranties?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We work with suppliers to establish clear return and warranty policies that meet UK consumer expectations while being fair to all parties. Typically, we handle minor returns through our own processes but coordinate with suppliers on larger warranty issues or product defects. Our goal is to minimize returns through quality product selection and clear consumer communication.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>What is your shipping and logistics process?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We operate a streamlined logistics system from our UK warehouse facilities. Our process includes:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Coordinating inbound shipments from suppliers</li>
                                <li>Quality control inspection upon receipt</li>
                                <li>Inventory management and storage</li>
                                <li>Order processing for various retail channels</li>
                                <li>Packaging and outbound shipping to retailers or direct to consumers</li>
                                <li>Returns processing and management</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>We work with reliable shipping partners to ensure efficient delivery throughout the UK and internationally when required.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                        <div class="faq-question">
                            <h3>How do you manage inventory and forecasting?</h3>
                            <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                        </div>
                        <div class="faq-answer">
                            <p>We use advanced inventory management systems and data analytics to optimize stock levels and forecast demand. Our approach includes:</p>
                            <ul>
                                <li>Regular sales data analysis across all channels</li>
                                <li>Seasonal demand forecasting</li>
                                <li>Just-in-time inventory management to minimize carrying costs</li>
                                <li>Proactive communication with suppliers about upcoming needs</li>
                                <li>Demand planning for promotional periods and peak seasons</li>
                            </ul>
                            <p>This systematic approach ensures we maintain optimal inventory levels while minimizing stockouts and overstock situations.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

                <h2 class="section-title">About The Blacksmith Market</h2>
                <div class="title-underline"></div>
                <p class="section-description">We specialize in identifying high-potential branded products and connecting them with the most profitable retail channels through data-driven market analysis.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="about-content">

                </div>
                <div class="about-text animate-on-scroll">
                    <h3>Our Product Selection Process</h3>
                    <p>With extensive experience in retail distribution, we've developed a rigorous methodology for selecting branded products that meet market demand and deliver consistent sales performance.</p>
                    <div class="feature-list">

                            </div>

                    </div>

                    <div class="timeline-number">03</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">

                    <div class="timeline-number">04</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">

                    </div>

                    <div class="timeline-number">05</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">
                        <h3>Performance Review</h3>

                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="timeline-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="timeline-number">06</div>
                    <div class="timeline-content">

                        <i class="fas fa-box"></i>
                    </div>

                        <i class="fas fa-sync-alt"></i>

                        <i class="fas fa-expand-arrows-alt"></i>

            <div class="faq-container">
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What retail channels do you distribute through?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We distribute products through multiple channels including online marketplaces (Amazon, eBay), specialty retailers, independent shops, and direct-to-consumer platforms. Our multi-channel approach allows us to place products where they're most likely to succeed based on category, price point, and target audience.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What are your typical order quantities?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>Our order quantities vary by product category, seasonality, and sales velocity. Initial orders typically range from 50-200 units per SKU for testing market response. For established products with proven sales, our regular orders can range from 200-1,000+ units depending on category and sales volume.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What are your payment terms?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We typically work with standard industry payment terms of Net 30 or Net 60 days. For new suppliers, we may start with a deposit and balance payment structure until the relationship is established. Long-term partners may qualify for more favorable terms as our relationship develops.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>Do you require exclusive distribution rights?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>While we don't require exclusivity for all products, we may discuss exclusive arrangements for select categories or channels where we can demonstrate significant market penetration and sales potential. These arrangements are negotiated on a case-by-case basis to ensure they benefit both parties.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>How do you handle product returns and warranties?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We work with suppliers to establish clear return and warranty policies that meet UK consumer expectations while being fair to all parties. Typically, we handle minor returns through our own processes but coordinate with suppliers on larger warranty issues or product defects.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="faq-item animate-on-scroll">
                    <div class="faq-question">
                        <h3>What documentation do you need from suppliers?</h3>
                        <i class="fas fa-chevron-down"></i>
                    </div>
                    <div class="faq-answer">
                        <p>We require standard product documentation including detailed specifications, high-resolution images, safety certifications relevant to the UK market (e.g., CE/UKCA marking), user manuals, and any required compliance documentation. For international suppliers, we also need export documentation and proof of ethical manufacturing practices.</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </section>

            <h1>Privacy Policy</h1>
            <nav aria-label="breadcrumb">
                <ol class="breadcrumb">
